2026-06-02T22:25:38+01:00 TAC-096 completed: added experiments/benchmark_content_update_frequency.py and tests_py/test_content_update_frequency.py. Initial broad artifact content_update_frequency_local_2026_06_02 was marked invalid for capability conclusions because it evaluated raw query logits after training the promoted memory adapter. Corrected adapter-aware matrix completed in runs/benchmarks/content_update_frequency_local_adapter_2026_06_02 across 5 chunked-recall tasks x 3 seeds x 8 schedules at 120 steps. Verdict: query_skip exactly matches full_update carry accuracy 0.1778, carry-reset delta 0.1667, carry-shuffled delta 0.1694, and content hit 0.1523, while improving query TPS ratio to 1.083. No-content updates collapse carry to 0.0153 and content hit to 0.0. Segment_every_8 is a strong positive-control candidate (carry 0.2014, TPS ratio 1.192, context update fraction 0.125) but is task-dependent: it helps single_key/delayed_query/noisy_key and hurts multi_key. Conclusion: a plain forced carried-state LM loss is not enough; the next bottleneck is the bridge from identity memory/readout into answer logits plus localized program causality. Verification passed for forced-identity unittest, py_compile, benchmark run, artifact json.tool, and prd.json json.tool.
